  ios-regex '_21576_',
  ios-regex '_3356_',
  ios-regex '_1239_',
  ios-regex '_7911_',
  ios-regex '_7132_',
  ios-regex '_701_',

!
route-policy PASS
  pass
end-policy
!
route-policy IC_ITESM
  if (destination in IC_ITESM) then
    set community (8151:635)
  endif
end-policy
!
route-policy TRANS_INT
  if (destination in MAS_24) then
    pass
  elseif (community matches-every 5) then
    set local-preference 100
    set community (8151:299, 8151:278) additive
  elseif (community matches-every 6) then
    set local-preference 98
    set community (8151:299, 8151:278) additive
  elseif (community matches-every 7) then
    set local-preference 96
    set community (8151:299, 8151:278) additive
  elseif (community matches-every 8) then
    set local-preference 94
    set community (8151:299, 8151:278) additive
  endif
end-policy
!
route-policy AS-PATH-99
  if (as-path in AS_CARRIERS_PEERS) then
    drop
  else
    pass
  endif
end-policy
!
route-policy DUAL_HOMED
  if (community matches-every 1) then
    set local-preference 100
    set community (no-export) additive
  elseif (community matches-every 2) then
    set local-preference 98
    set community (no-export) additive
  elseif (community matches-every 3) then
    set local-preference 96
    set community (no-export) additive
  elseif (community matches-every 4) then
    set local-preference 94
    set community (no-export) additive
  elseif (community matches-every 5) then
    set local-preference 100
  elseif (community matches-every 6) then
    set local-preference 98
  elseif (community matches-every 7) then
    set local-preference 96
  elseif (community matches-every 8) then
    set local-preference 94
  else
    pass
  endif
end-policy
!
route-policy MAXAS_LIMIT
  if (as-path length ge 31) then
    drop
  else
    pass
  endif
end-policy
!
route-policy SAMECLUSTER
  if ((community matches-any SAMECLUSTER) and (destination in RUTA_CERO)) then
    pass
  elseif ((community matches-any TERCERRESPALDO) and (destination in RUTA_CERO)) then
    set local-preference 50
  elseif (destination in RUTA_CERO) then
    drop
  else
    pass
  endif
end-policy
!
route-policy IC_CABLEOPER
  if (destination in IC_CABLEOPER) then
    pass
  endif
end-policy
!
route-policy MARCA_REGION
  set community (8151:656) additive
end-policy
!
route-policy OTHERCLUSTER
  if (community matches-any 99) then
    drop
  elseif ((community matches-any SEGUNDORESPALDO) and (destination in RUTA_CERO)) then
    set local-preference 75
  elseif (destination in RUTA_CERO) then
    drop
  else
    pass
  endif
end-policy
!
route-policy SERIALES_MEXICO
  if (destination in 1) then
    set community (8151:277, 8151:279, no-export)
  endif
end-policy
!
route-policy BGP_MARCA_IPS_00
  if (destination in BGP_IPS_00_UNINET) then
    set local-preference 100
    set community (8151:277, no-export) additive
  elseif (destination in BGP_IPS_00_CLIENTE) then
    set local-preference 100
    set community (8151:278) additive
  endif
end-policy
!
route-policy BGP_IPV4_CORPORATIVO
  if (destination in CORPORATIVO) then
    apply DUAL_HOMED
  endif
end-policy
!
route-policy ESTATICAS_CLIENTES_IDE
  if (destination in RTBHR) then
    drop
  elseif (destination in REDES_PRIVADAS) then
    set community (no-export)
  elseif (destination in ESTATICAS_IPS_UNINET) then
    set community (8151:277, no-export)
  elseif (destination in ESTATICAS_IPS_CLIENTE) then
    set community (8151:278)
  elseif (destination in 1) then
    pass
  endif
end-policy
!
route-policy BGP_IPV4_CICESE_ECOSUR_SUB50
  if (destination in CICESE_ECOSUR_SUB50) then
    apply BGP_MARCA_IPS_00
  endif
end-policy
!
route-policy DH_IPV4_UNIDAD_DEPORTIVA_SEDEM
  if (destination in UNIDAD_DEPORTIVA_SEDEM) then
    apply DUAL_HOMED
  endif
end-policy
!
route-policy IC_UNACH_TUXTLA_CENTRAL_BGP_MARCA_IPS_00
  if (destination in IC_UNACH_TUXTLA_CENTRAL) then
    apply BGP_MARCA_IPS_00
  endif
end-policy
!
route-policy DH_IPV4_CENTRO_DE_CONVENCIONES_Y_POLYFORUM
  if (destination in IC_CENTRO_DE_CONVENCIONES_Y_POLYFORUM) then
    apply DUAL_HOMED
  endif
end-policy
!
route-policy DH_IPV4_CENTRO_DE_CONVENCIONES_Y_POLYFORUM_02
  if (destination in CENTRO_DE_CONVENCIONES_Y_POLYFORUM) then
    apply DUAL_HOMED
  endif
end-policy
